\DoxyCodeLine{46 }
\DoxyCodeLine{47 \textcolor{comment}{// Throw `out\_of\_range` from `toml::value::at()` and `toml::find()`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{comment}{// after generating an error message.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{// The implementation is a bit complicated and there are many edge-\/cases.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{// If you are not interested in the error message generation, just skip this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Value>}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 [[noreturn]] \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_1_1detail_aeeb2c5b93a35ab7ab068c8479e5dd54f}{throw\_key\_not\_found\_error}}(\textcolor{keyword}{const} Value\& v, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_ab00c292fbb2e761ef69fdafd6b813348}{key}}\& ky)}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{56     \textcolor{comment}{// The top-\/level table has its region at the first character of the file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57     \textcolor{comment}{// That means that, in the case when a key is not found in the top-\/level}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58     \textcolor{comment}{// table, the error message points to the first character. If the file has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59     \textcolor{comment}{// its first table at the first line, the error message would be like this.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60     \textcolor{comment}{// ```console}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61     \textcolor{comment}{// [error] key "{}a"{} not found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62     \textcolor{comment}{//  -\/-\/> example.toml}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63     \textcolor{comment}{//    |}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64     \textcolor{comment}{//  1 | [table]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65     \textcolor{comment}{//    | \string^-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ in this table}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66     \textcolor{comment}{// ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67     \textcolor{comment}{// It actually points to the top-\/level table at the first character,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68     \textcolor{comment}{// not `[table]`. But it is too confusing. To avoid the confusion, the error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69     \textcolor{comment}{// message should explicitly say "{}key not found in the top-\/level table"{},}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70     \textcolor{comment}{// or "{}the parsed file is empty"{} if there is no content at all (0 bytes in file).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keyword}{auto} loc = v.location();}
\DoxyCodeLine{72     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(loc.line() == 1 \&\& loc.region() == 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{73     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{74         \textcolor{comment}{// First line with a zero-\/length region means "{}empty file"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75         \textcolor{comment}{// The region will be generated at `parse\_toml\_file` function}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76         \textcolor{comment}{// if the file contains no bytes.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77         \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} std::out\_of\_range(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_1_1detail_ada573c450f0429aedaae47101e581ac8}{format\_underline}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_adea2ccfef76e94dc32396c306a550c27}{concat\_to\_string}}(}
\DoxyCodeLine{78             \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}key \(\backslash\)"{}"{}}, ky, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)"{} not found in the top-\/level table"{}}), \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{79                 \{loc, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}the parsed file is empty"{}}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80             \}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{81     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(loc.line() == 1 \&\& loc.region() == 1)}
\DoxyCodeLine{83     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{84         \textcolor{comment}{// Here it assumes that top-\/level table starts at the first character.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85         \textcolor{comment}{// The region corresponds to the top-\/level table will be generated at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86         \textcolor{comment}{// `parse\_toml\_file` function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87         \textcolor{comment}{//     It also assumes that the top-\/level table size is just one and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88         \textcolor{comment}{// the line number is `1`. It is always satisfied. And those conditions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89         \textcolor{comment}{// are satisfied only if the table is the top-\/level table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91         \textcolor{comment}{// 1. one-\/character dot-\/key at the first line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92         \textcolor{comment}{// ```toml}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93         \textcolor{comment}{// a.b = "{}c"{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94         \textcolor{comment}{// ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95         \textcolor{comment}{// toml11 counts whole key as the table key. Here, `a.b` is the region}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96         \textcolor{comment}{// of the table "{}a"{}. It could be counter intuitive, but it works.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97         \textcolor{comment}{// The size of the region is 3, not 1. The above example is the shortest}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98         \textcolor{comment}{// dot-\/key example. The size cannot be 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100         \textcolor{comment}{// 2. one-\/character inline-\/table at the first line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101         \textcolor{comment}{// ```toml}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102         \textcolor{comment}{// a = \{b = "{}c"{}\}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103         \textcolor{comment}{// ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104         \textcolor{comment}{// toml11 considers the inline table body as the table region. Here,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105         \textcolor{comment}{// `\{b = "{}c"{}\}` is the region of the table "{}a"{}. The size of the region}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106         \textcolor{comment}{// is 9, not 1. The shotest inline table still has two characters, `\{`}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107         \textcolor{comment}{// and `\}`. The size cannot be 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109         \textcolor{comment}{// 3. one-\/character table declaration at the first line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110         \textcolor{comment}{// ```toml}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111         \textcolor{comment}{// [a]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112         \textcolor{comment}{// ```}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113         \textcolor{comment}{// toml11 considers the whole table key as the table region. Here,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{114         \textcolor{comment}{// `[a]` is the table region. The size is 3, not 1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{115         \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{116         \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} std::out\_of\_range(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_1_1detail_ada573c450f0429aedaae47101e581ac8}{format\_underline}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_adea2ccfef76e94dc32396c306a550c27}{concat\_to\_string}}(}
\DoxyCodeLine{117             \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}key \(\backslash\)"{}"{}}, ky, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)"{} not found in the top-\/level table"{}}), \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{118                 \{loc, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}the top-\/level table starts here"{}}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{119             \}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{120     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{121     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{122     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{123         \textcolor{comment}{// normal table.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{124         \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw} std::out\_of\_range(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_1_1detail_ada573c450f0429aedaae47101e581ac8}{format\_underline}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetoml_adea2ccfef76e94dc32396c306a550c27}{concat\_to\_string}}(}
\DoxyCodeLine{125             \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}key \(\backslash\)"{}"{}}, ky, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)"{} not found"{}}), \{ \{loc, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}in this table"{}}\} \}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{126     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{127 \}}
